## Actor Model

*Libraries for building actor-based programs.*

* [ProtoActor](https://github.com/asynkron/protoactor-go) ‚≠ê 5,372 | üêõ 57 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-28 - Proto Actor - Ultra fast distributed actors for Go, C# and Java/Kotlin.
* [Ergo](https://github.com/ergo-services/ergo) ‚≠ê 4,240 | üêõ 5 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-29 - An actor-based Framework with network transparency for creating event-driven architecture in Golang. Inspired by Erlang.
* [Hollywood](https://github.com/anthdm/hollywood) ‚≠ê 2,081 | üêõ 21 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-07-04 - Blazingly fast and light-weight Actor engine written in Golang.
* [Goakt](https://github.com/Tochemey/goakt) ‚≠ê 294 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-31 - Fast and Distributed Actor framework using protocol buffers as message for Golang.
* [asyncmachine-go/pkg/machine](https://github.com/pancsta/asyncmachine-go/tree/main/pkg/machine) ‚≠ê 155 | üêõ 23 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-19 - Graph control flow library (AOP, actor, state-machine).

## Artificial Intelligence

*Libraries for building programs that leverage AI.*

* [Ollama](https://github.com/jmorganca/ollama) ‚≠ê 155,133 | üêõ 2,234 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-31 - Run large language models locally.
* [LocalAI](https://github.com/mudler/LocalAI) ‚≠ê 36,177 | üêõ 295 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-31 - Open Source OpenAI alternative, self-host AI models.
* [langchaingo](https://github.com/tmc/langchaingo) ‚≠ê 7,909 | üêõ 360 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-20 - LangChainGo is a framework for developing applications powered by language models.
* [chromem-go](https://github.com/philippgille/chromem-go) ‚≠ê 752 | üêõ 14 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-10 - Embeddable vector database for Go with Chroma-like interface and zero third-party dependencies. In-memory with optional persistence.
* [OllamaFarm](https://github.com/presbrey/ollamafarm) ‚≠ê 91 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-02-01 - Manage, load-balance, and failover packs of Ollamas.
* [fun](https://gitlab.com/tozd/go/fun) - The simplest but powerful way to use large language models (LLMs) in Go.

## Audio and Music

*Libraries for manipulating audio.*

* [beep](https://github.com/faiface/beep) ‚≠ê 2,170 | üêõ 75 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-03-19 - A simple library for playback and audio manipulation.
* [Oto](https://github.com/hajimehoshi/oto) ‚≠ê 1,811 | üêõ 26 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-21 - A low-level library to play sound on multiple platforms.
* [PortAudio](https://github.com/gordonklaus/portaudio) ‚≠ê 805 | üêõ 7 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-02-06 - Go bindings for the PortAudio audio I/O library.
* [play](https://github.com/paololazzari/play) ‚≠ê 495 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-03-28 - Command-line audio player that supports multiple formats including WAV, MP3, OGG, and FLAC.
* [GoAudio](https://github.com/DylanMeeus/GoAudio) ‚≠ê 390 | üêõ 10 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-04-23 - Native Go Audio Processing Library.
* [malgo](https://github.com/gen2brain/malgo) ‚≠ê 356 | üêõ 9 | üåê C | üìÖ 2025-09-19 - Mini audio library.
* [id3v2](https://github.com/bogem/id3v2) ‚≠ê 354 | üêõ 25 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-10-28 - ID3 decoding and encoding library for Go.
* [flac](https://github.com/mewkiz/flac) ‚≠ê 344 | üêõ 8 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-08-18 - Native Go FLAC encoder/decoder with support for FLAC streams.
* [gaad](https://github.com/Comcast/gaad) ‚≠ê 134 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-01-27 - Native Go AAC bitstream parser.
* [minimp3](https://github.com/tosone/minimp3) ‚≠ê 132 | üêõ 3 | üåê C | üìÖ 2025-07-09 - Lightweight MP3 decoder library.
* [gosamplerate](https://github.com/dh1tw/gosamplerate) ‚≠ê 37 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-01-28 - libsamplerate bindings for go.

## Authentication and Authorization

*Libraries for implementing authentication and authorization.*

* [casbin](https://github.com/hsluoyz/casbin) ‚≠ê 19,345 | üêõ 21 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-11-01 - Authorization library that supports access control models like ACL, RBAC, and ABAC.
* [jwt-go](https://github.com/golang-jwt/jwt) ‚≠ê 8,630 | üêõ 47 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-13 - A full featured implementation of JSON Web Tokens (JWT). This library supports the parsing and verification as well as the generation and signing of JWTs.
* [goth](https://github.com/markbates/goth) ‚≠ê 6,290 | üêõ 133 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-09 - provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to use OAuth and OAuth2. Handles multiple providers out of the box.
* [spicedb](https://github.com/authzed/spicedb) ‚≠ê 6,156 | üêõ 130 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-31 - A Zanzibar-inspired database that enables fine-grained authorization.
* [oauth2](https://github.com/golang/oauth2) ‚≠ê 5,727 | üêõ 49 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-23 - Successor of goauth2. Generic OAuth 2.0 package that comes with JWT, Google APIs, Compute Engine, and App Engine support.
* [keto](https://github.com/ory/keto) ‚≠ê 5,159 | üêõ 58 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-31 - Open Source (Go) implementation of "Zanzibar: Google's Consistent, Global Authorization System". Ships gRPC, REST APIs, newSQL, and an easy and granular permission language. Supports ACL, RBAC, and other access models.
* [openfga](https://github.com/openfga/openfga) ‚≠ê 4,313 | üêõ 148 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-31 - Implementation of fine-grained authorization based on the "Zanzibar: Google's Consistent, Global Authorization System" paper. Backed by [CNCF](https://www.cncf.io/).
* [authboss](https://github.com/volatiletech/authboss) ‚≠ê 4,092 | üêõ 38 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-09-09 - Modular authentication system for the web. It tries to remove as much boilerplate and "hard things" as possible so that each time you start a new web project in Go, you can plug it in, configure it, and start building your app without having to build an authentication system each time.
* [scs](https://github.com/alexedwards/scs) ‚≠ê 2,452 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-02 - Session Manager for HTTP servers.
* [jwx](https://github.com/lestrrat-go/jwx) ‚≠ê 2,247 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-11-01 - Go module implementing various JWx (JWA/JWE/JWK/JWS/JWT, otherwise known as JOSE) technologies.
* [osin](https://github.com/openshift/osin) ‚≠ê 1,932 | üêõ 3 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-09-08 - Golang OAuth2 server library.
* [loginsrv](https://github.com/tarent/loginsrv) ‚≠ê 1,929 | üêõ 27 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2021-02-27 - JWT login microservice with pluggable backends such as OAuth2 (Github), htpasswd, osiam.
* [gologin](https://github.com/dghubble/gologin) ‚≠ê 1,927 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-31 - chainable handlers for login with OAuth1 and OAuth2 authentication providers.
* [oidc](https://github.com/zitadel/oidc) ‚≠ê 1,698 | üêõ 28 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-15 - Easy to use OpenID Connect client and server library written for Go and certified by the OpenID Foundation.
* [gorbac](https://github.com/mikespook/gorbac) ‚≠ê 1,645 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-08-28 - provides a lightweight role-based access control (RBAC) implementation in Golang.
* [paseto](https://github.com/o1egl/paseto) ‚≠ê 915 | üêõ 7 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-02-25 - Golang implementation of Platform-Agnostic Security Tokens (PASETO).
* [jwt](https://github.com/cristalhq/jwt) ‚≠ê 688 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-06-22 - Safe, simple, and fast JSON Web Tokens for Go.
* [go-guardian](https://github.com/shaj13/go-guardian) ‚≠ê 597 | üêõ 12 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-07-25 - Go-Guardian is a golang library that provides a simple, clean, and idiomatic way to create powerful modern API and web authentication that supports LDAP, Basic, Bearer token, and Certificate based authentication.
* [go-jose](https://github.com/go-jose/go-jose) ‚≠ê 451 | üêõ 30 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-03 - Fairly complete implementation of the JOSE working group's JSON Web Token, JSON Web Signatures, and JSON Web Encryption specs.
* [jwt](https://github.com/pascaldekloe/jwt) ‚≠ê 363 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-04-29 - Lightweight JSON Web Token (JWT) library.
* [jeff](https://github.com/abraithwaite/jeff) ‚≠ê 270 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-01-23 - Simple, flexible, secure, and idiomatic web session management with pluggable backends.
* [gosession](https://github.com/Kwynto/gosession) ‚≠ê 256 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-07-31 - This is quick session for net/http in GoLang. This package is perhaps the best implementation of the session mechanism, or at least it tries to become one.
* [jwt-auth](https://github.com/adam-hanna/jwt-auth) ‚≠ê 235 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2021-08-01 - JWT middleware for Golang http servers with many configuration options.
* [goiabada](https://github.com/leodip/goiabada) ‚≠ê 157 | üêõ 6 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-09-11 - An open-source authentication and authorization server supporting OAuth2 and OpenID Connect.
* [otpgen](https://github.com/grijul/otpgen) ‚≠ê 140 | üêõ 1 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-01-17 - Library to generate TOTP/HOTP codes.
* [sessionup](https://github.com/swithek/sessionup) ‚≠ê 128 | üêõ 3 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-03-20 - Simple, yet effective HTTP session management and identification package.
* [sjwt](https://github.com/brianvoe/sjwt) ‚≠ê 122 | üêõ 1 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-02-01 - Simple jwt generator and parser.
* [session](https://github.com/icza/session) ‚≠ê 118 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2024-08-24 - Go session management for web servers (including support for Google App Engine - GAE).
* [branca](https://github.com/essentialkaos/branca) ‚≠ê 92 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-13 - branca token [specification implementation](https://github.com/tuupola/branca-spec) ‚≠ê 232 | üêõ 10 | üìÖ 2025-05-06 for Golang 1.15+.
* [securecookie](https://github.com/chmike/securecookie) ‚≠ê 83 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-02-18 - Efficient secure cookie encoding/decoding.
* [sessions](https://github.com/adam-hanna/sessions) ‚≠ê 78 | üêõ 4 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2023-07-17 - Dead simple, highly performant, highly customizable sessions service for go http servers.
* [otpgo](https://github.com/jltorresm/otpgo) ‚≠ê 75 | üêõ 2 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2021-02-27 - Time-Based One-Time Password (TOTP) and HMAC-Based One-Time Password (HOTP) library for Go.
* [scope](https://github.com/SonicRoshan/scope) ‚≠ê 42 | üêõ 1 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2021-05-25 - Easily Manage OAuth2 Scopes In Go.
* [go-githubauth](https://github.com/jferrl/go-githubauth) ‚≠ê 26 | üêõ 0 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-10-28 - Utilities for GitHub authentication: generate and use GitHub application and installation tokens.

### Project Layout

***Unofficial** set of patterns for structuring projects.*

* [golang-standards/project-layout](https://github.com/golang-standards/project-layout) ‚≠ê 54,276 | üêõ 95 | üåê Makefile | üìÖ 2025-10-09 - Set of common historical and emerging project layout patterns in the Go ecosystem. ## Natural Language Processing

*Libraries for working with human languages.*

See also [Text Processing](#text-processing) and [Text Analysis](#text-analysis).

### Language Detection

* [lingua-go](https://github.com/pemistahl/lingua-go) ‚≠ê 1,288 | üêõ 9 | üåê Go | üìÖ 2025-02-06 - An accurate natural language detection library, suitable for long and short text alike. Supports detecting multiple languages in mixed-language text.

### HTTP Clients

## E-Books

### E-books for purchase

* [Go in Practice, Second Edition](https://www.manning.com/books/go-in-practice-second-edition) - Your practical guide on the ins-and-outs of Go development, covering the standard library and the most important tools from Go‚Äôs powerful ecosystem.
* [Know Go: Generics](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/generics) - A guide to understanding and using generics in Go.
* [Lets-Go](https://lets-go.alexedwards.net) - A step-by-step guide to creating fast, secure and maintanable web applications with Go.
* [Lets-Go-Further](https://lets-go-further.alexedwards.net) - Advanced patterns for building APIs and web applications in Go.
* [The Power of Go: Tests](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/tests) - A guide to testing in Go.
* [The Power of Go: Tools](https://bitfieldconsulting.com/books/tools) - A guide to writing command-line tools in Go.
* [Writing A Compiler In Go](https://compilerbook.com)
* [Writing An Interpreter In Go](https://interpreterbook.com) - Book that introduces dozens of techniques for writing idiomatic, expressive, and efficient Go code that avoids common pitfalls.
